   \n                    }\n                });\n                PH.cookie.set(\'voucher_notification\',\'\',-1,\'/\',window.cookie_domain || EM.cookie_domain);\n            }catch(e){\n            }\n        }        \n    })\n</script></div>\n    </div>\n</nav>\n    <nav id="auxiliary" class="navbar navbar-aux adjust-on-modal hidden-xs">\n    <div class="container">\n        <div
